Different lines arrive at more than a dozen ports of entry to visit small scenic spots and check in. Shentan Road is a relatively large and popular port of entry. Xixuan Hotel has a sense of design. The three-story building has a multi-dimensional and layered layout of the space, combining the western minimalist style and the Japanese courtyard style ingeniously. There is a large space in the lobby as a stepped tea room. The left and right stairs are connected by a small air corridor. Under the corridor is a courtyard waterscape created by a shallow pool, which is obviously used as a dry landscape to create an artistic conception. The room is also split-level design, the bed is on the lower level, and there is a desk and tea set on the upper level, the space layout is very unique. The bed is average in comfort but adequate for lying on. The floor has obvious signs of wear and tear but is within the normal range. The bathroom is generally clean and complete with supplies, but there is some dirt on the shower and floor drain that cannot be scrubbed off. These are related to the age of the opening and decoration. It is recommended to invest in maintenance and arrangement to improve the guest experience. What happened: My husband was on a business trip. I was muttering in my heart and trying to figure out how to open it. It wasn't until my daughter started crying out of fear that I realized that the door lock was actually broken! ! Can't open the door in the bathroom! Accompanied by the cries of my daughter getting louder and louder, and when I touched my pocket and found that the phone was not with me, I was terrified at the time (parents should understand my feelings), talking loudly to my daughter, and again Remind her to be alone outside the bathroom, just stand in the doorway, and not run to that floor-to-ceiling glass I mentioned earlier, while trying to stay calm! I knew my daughter was outside the door alone, and I couldn't let her stay for too long, the longer the risk, the higher the risk. Later, I saw the emergency call next to the toilet, but fortunately it was not broken! ! Dial the front desk! ! ! After making the phone call, while pretending to calmly comfort my daughter while waiting for rescue, only I know the fear inside! What I am afraid of is not how long I will be locked up, but whether the four-and-a-half-year-old child outside the door will be in danger! ! Finally, the person who opened the door for us came! Although my daughter was terrified of crying, but fortunately, God bless her, she didn't run around! (Later, I didn‚Äôt know until the repairman came, and I heard a click, that the door could be opened from the outside, that is to say, it couldn‚Äôt be opened from the inside)
I was shaking with anger! ! It's obviously not broken, so why can't the inside be opened to the outside? ? Is this reasonable? ? Why give it to guests without checking? ? Is it a careless omission or no inspection at all? ? In the event of a fire, what should a guest staying alone do? ? Is this just my room or is this the case in all hotel rooms? ?
The most, most, and most angry thing is that I found out that in 22.5 months, some guests wrote that they were locked inside because of the door problem! ! Then why did such a thing happen after more than half a year? ? ?
Really disappointed, simply black-hearted, too weak sense of responsibility!
